1)
Total Restoration Ceremony
When the fall occurred, (drawing a diagram on the blackboard) it fell away from here, so the restoration age must rise in the opposite direction. 
That is why this is always the position of Adam and Eve, and in Christian terms, this is the concept of the Second Coming. This is to establish a family centered on a true man or a true woman, and through the national form and the ethnic form connected to that family, we must carry out the indemnity condition that turns this around. 
The reason for resolving grievances and the people who must resolve them
So what must be done to return? God must not have grievances. Although God has been carrying out the restoration history for fallen humanity, we cannot return with God's sad position until now. Therefore, we must carry out a restoration ceremony to resolve grievances.
Furthermore, we have gone through three eras from the time of Adam to the time of Jesus and now to the time of the Second Coming. Now, the true parents who can stand in the position of parents must not have grievances. They must not have grievances against the enemy or against this earth. 
We must resolve all of this. Then what must be done? Only when the grievances of the parents are resolved can God's grievances ultimately be resolved. Therefore, for God's grievances to be resolved, the grievances of the parents must be resolved. Only after the true parents come out and can resolve all grievances can God's grievances be resolved. Only after resolving God's grievances and the grievances of the parents can we resolve all grievances of the tribe, nation, country, and world. This is how it works. 
Connecting the Spiritual Christian Realm to the Physical Christian Realm in the Unification Church
So what kind of ceremony should we hold today? Until now, the restoration history has been a history that has paved the foundation for the Messiah, that is, the parents, to come since the day Cain and Abel were separated. Just as the historical form has grown from the infant stage to the boyhood stage, youth stage, and adulthood stage, in the restoration age, many Abels have been sacrificed to widen that path. This must be formed up to the national standard. The parents, that is, the one who becomes the Messiah, must appear as a representative based on the national standard.
Based on this standard, the foundation of Abel's history has been expanded nationally, which is the nation of Israel and Judaism. The one who came to this earth to have a royal authority based on the foundation of Judaism and the nation of Israel is the Messiah, that is, Jesus. However, due to Jesus' death, Christianity was restored a second time. However, Christianity is only spiritual. It has not been established in both spirit and body.
That is why today, the problem for our Unification Church is how to connect the spiritual Christian realm to the physical Christian realm. This has been the mission of the teacher until now. Therefore, from 1970 to 1972, based on the spiritual standard, we have taken a leading position in the Republic of Korea. We have stood in the mainstream of the Republic of Korea and presented the direction of all national fortunes, connecting that standard spiritually to the global Christianity from 1972 to 1974. We must connect the form of Christianity in the spiritual world to the physical national standard. Since Jesus died based on the physical national standard, we must come into the Republic of Korea in 1975 and connect this standard to the form of Israel based on the physical national standard.
Therefore, events such as the banquet in January, the wedding in February, and the international mobilization in April are mobilizing everything in a short period of time. At the banquet, the teacher must appear before this nation and many prominent figures. Then, our families, the blessed families, must appear before the world. That is how our joint wedding becomes known to the world. After that, the members of our Unification Church must appear before the people of the world. Because there is a historical indemnity period, this year, until the end of April, according to the lunar calendar, which does not go beyond May in the solar calendar, is the period to completely indemnify everything.
Finally, because this time has come, the teacher has appeared in the Republic of Korea for the first time in his life. When appearing before the nation, one must appear with authority. Then, we have revealed our family before the nation and the whole world, and then we have done this work of revealing all the members of our Unification Church to the world. We must work based on this national standard, which is God's will.
Therefore, due to this revival conference, what phenomenon will occur? The entire nation will focus its attention on us. This will become a major historical event.
Then, looking at the time of Jesus, although Judaism and Rome united to kill Jesus, now the times have changed and must be reversed. The Unification Church and our Republic of Korea must unite as one. Currently, Christianity is opposing us. The emergence of such a phenomenon indicates that it is the time when the principled standards of the historical indemnity restoration age are aligning.
That is why the police do not even know why they are helping in such a way. Moreover, they cannot help but do so because they have brought the fortunes of the world from various countries, and if they do not accept them based on the national standard, they will be caught in conditions. Also, even when we look at the policy aspect of the flat earthly world, if the people from these 25 countries come here and suffer harm, it will become a global political issue. It will immediately become a condition for reporting to the country through the embassy, so they have no choice but to welcome us. Thus, the entire Republic of Korea is guiding us, and the police are all supporting us, and the whole country is moving in our favor. This symbolizes the complete integration of the national standard centered on the principles of indemnity restoration in both spirit and body.
The Significance and Method of the Total Restoration Ceremony
Today, when we look at this association, it is the 21st anniversary of the founding of the association and the last period of the second seven-year course. This is because it started in April. Also, if we look at the teacher's own life, it is a time that exceeds 30 years.
In such an era, we must carry out the total restoration ceremony of all things. When holding this ceremony, we must first perform the restoration ceremony before God. After that, we must perform the restoration ceremony for the true parents. Then, what does it mean that Teacher Choi is celebrating his 60th birthday? It means to return again. In other words, it means to return through restoration. Teacher Choi's 60th birthday is a return, but centered on Teacher Choi, we can stand in the position of a true woman of the fallen world, like a mother, and indemnify all of the new restoration history. Now everything will change centered on Teacher Choi. The fallen world, the entire spiritual world must be indemnified centered on Teacher Choi. It is not about indemnifying centered on the original parents. In the original world, where the parents are good and complete, the conditions for the fall do not establish.
Of course, the teacher has cleared everything, but ultimately, because the woman made a mistake, we must gather all of this together and indemnify it. So what must be done? Teacher Choi must completely indemnify and cross over, and he cannot do it alone. We must unify all the numerous religions, including Christianity, Islam, Buddhism, Confucianism, and all of them. Then, in the historical era, there have been good kings and loyal subjects. Among the loyal subjects, there were civil and military officials. Centered on each nation, the good kings and loyal subjects must all unite and cross over.
Next, we must unify those who have not believed in religion but have stood in a conscientious position. Heaven has testified, but there are those who do not serve God's will. These people include philosophers and conscientious individuals. We must unify all such people. Furthermore, we must also include the Cain-like world, which connects from Lucifer to Judas Iscariot, from Emperor Nero to the current communist world, and open the way for the conditions of indemnity. We must open the way to save even the communists and bind them all together so that on this day, they all submit and declare that they will follow the heavenly principle.
Thus, we must connect everything centered on Teacher Choi and carry out the total restoration of all things. Under such a foundation, the liberation of the parents and the liberation of God will occur.
Now, we have prepared a table. What does this table signify? There are spirits of those who have believed in our Unification Church until now. We must also restore those Unification Church members. Here, there are also Hee-jin, Hye-jin, and those who have passed away. We must spiritually restore all those who have believed in the Unification Church, including the president of the association and those who have passed away. Many people have left the Unification Church, and we must connect all of them and indemnify them.
Now, when we set the table, if this is God, then the next will be Christianity centered on Jesus. The next will be the religious people who have believed in religion, followed by philosophers and conscientious individuals, then the kings, good kings, and loyal subjects, and finally the Cain-like world. It all fits in. The table must originally be arranged in the four directions of east, west, south, and north. There is also the angelic world. We must also restore the angelic world.
We must place religious people centered on Christianity in the east, the angelic world in the west, the good kings and patriotic ancestors in the south, and the Cain-like satanic world in the north. This is how we must carry out the total restoration. Therefore, what day is today? It is the day of total restoration, a day for the total restoration ceremony in history. By coming out on this day, we will cross over. From now on, the laws of heaven will be established. Until now, many religions, including Christianity, have followed this path without knowing it, but through this transitional ceremony, from now on, the laws will be established centered on the Unification Church.
To establish a global foundation, we must fight and win against communism.
Even in the spirit world, they can no longer act recklessly. Until now, evil spirits have applied the law of indemnity as they pleased, but that will no longer be the case. They can establish conditions of indemnity only through their lineage and the relative earthly people corresponding to their conscientious standards. That does not become an overreach. Thus, order will be established. Do you understand? From now on, the establishment of the constitution of the heavenly kingdom will begin.
Now, in three years, the teacher must connect the physical foundation established in Korea to the democratic world represented by the United States. On the day this ends, the entire world will enter a time when God can directly intervene. At that time, they will not be able to oppose the Unification Church. Some will die of heart attacks from opposing it, and some will die in their sleep; all kinds of people will emerge. In the past, evil spirits did all sorts of tricks to control the evil authority of this earth. Just like giving medicine and causing illness, now the good side will enter a time when it can unilaterally punish.
This period extends until 1977 and 1978. We must establish the substantial national foundation in the United States before this period ends. Just as the Republic of Korea supports us today, if the United States can come forward and support the whole, the world will completely transition into God's will. While this is the case on a national standard, to establish a global foundation, we must fight against communism. Thus, this time, all fortunes are opposed to both communism and us. The Republic of Korea is currently facing North Korea, and of course, President Park is currently at the forefront, but ultimately, we are not united. Japan is also opposing us. That is why the conflict with Ishihara centered on Minobe is happening, and currently, in the United States, there is a struggle against communism.
Therefore, ultimately, the issue is how to push through the brutal counterattack of the communists over these three years and draw the United States into the heavenly side beyond the encirclement of communism. You must understand that this remains in the upcoming three-year course. If such a standard is established, God's will will be applied anywhere in the world.
Now, as we move toward the global stage centered on the spiritual and physical standards of indemnity, looking at the national standard, the restoration history until now has been a vertical history. Therefore, looking at the current national standard, the nation will finally become a base with a form to go to the world. Do you understand? Until now, because this has been a game of rising, if it fails to rise, it falls down. If it falls down, it must be re-indemnified down to the bottom.
Therefore, Christianity has come out with a rehash of what Judaism got wrong. Similarly, we are trying to restore not only the spiritual standards set by Christianity but also the physical standards, aiming to transcend national boundaries centered on this day. We must recognize that today is such an amazing day. From now on, it is time to use this point as a foundation to reach out to the world.

Just as Jesus began Christianity with 120 disciples under a global foundation, our Unification Church today is sending out missionaries in groups of three centered around 120 countries. By April of this year, or at the latest by mid-May, all will be sent out.

We must open the path for missions in 120 countries this year to spread the form of the three disciples centered on Jesus across the world. Only then can the national standards we are establishing relate to the global horizontal foundation, allowing all spirits to return and cooperate in the world. Thus, we cannot do without national standards. Only by comprehensively restoring these here can all spirits now freely operate on this earth as their stage of activity. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

<Prayer> Beloved Father, we know the sorrowful fact that you could not accomplish the great work of creation on this earth. Just as the mistake of Adam and Eve brought you grief and sorrow, we understand that you have labored to resolve that sorrowful grief. As we reflect on the countless good ancestors you have led and sacrificed, we thank you for establishing the connection of True Parents on this earth through a long history, centered on this land of Korea and this Unification Church.

Here, the sons and daughters present have been called before you to take responsibility and stand in this place. As we contemplate the immense suffering you endured on the path of restoration, we are aware of the deep sorrow you felt when Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, fell. Since the day we vowed to turn back from the path of betrayal to Heaven and pledge our loyalty for you, 30 years have passed since that time when we were born according to Heaven's will.

During this time, there have been internal struggles that no one could express or speak about. You alone know the heartache that has existed from your heart to the heart of this child today.

We earnestly desire to resolve your grief by transcending the limits of the nation. As we reflect on the amazing fact that May 1, 1975, is the day to resolve the grief of the tragic day when Jesus came to this earth and had to go to the cross, we thank you.

We have reached this significant time, marking the 21st anniversary of the founding of the church and the conclusion of the second seven-year course of restoration concerning global Christianity. When we view this ceremony, it also marks the conclusion of 30 years of history. When we consider that all of this has prepared the path for your restoration, we feel deeply humbled.

Father, we know the sorrow of that day when you faced the fallen ancestors of humanity, and the sorrow of having to send Jesus to fulfill your wishes, only to have him sacrificed on the cross. We also recognize the grief of countless Christians who followed him and were slaughtered, along with the many other religions that have sacrificed along their uncertain paths while seeking to honor Heaven.

We understand that the sorrow you felt for all those who were sacrificed in that process was immense. In the religious background, standing in the middle representing your name and your righteousness, the angels who were supposed to support the standard of completion with Adam and Eve were in a pitiful position and could not fulfill their role. We know they have sympathized with your heart and your will.

Now, Father, as you come to know that you have found the family of True Parents and the body of True Parents, this day, this son and this daughter are offered before you. Additionally, the children centered on this son and daughter are present in this place and in East Garden. Father, please accept us.

We thank you for allowing us to have a day when we can resolve the foundation of resentment lost due to the fall of the family, and for allowing us to offer this time before you, centered on this nation and people.

You also know that the twists and turns of the angelic world have grown due to the fall of the family. Father, please allow this day to be one where your heart is resolved through the restoration of True Parents, allowing the angels to also be restored.

Through the restoration of God, True Parents, and the angelic world, we connect the Christianity centered on Jesus, Confucianism and Confucius, Buddhism and Buddha, and the Islamic world and Muhammad, along with all the nations spread across the world. This ceremony is your restoration, the restoration of True Parents, and the restoration of the angelic world, allowing all religious people on this earth to achieve restoration. We thank you for allowing this connection to happen on this day.

By claiming the right of restoration of religion, a group has emerged that can now establish the sovereign authority of the Kingdom of God and praise you. In addition, many conscientious individuals, philosophers, and representatives from various nations, whether military or civilian, have become loyal subjects and sages, helping their nations advance toward the good heavenly kingdom, despite differing positions and environments.

On this joyful day, Father, please connect all the countless spirits who have helped in this process. Until now, they have been waiting in anguish, not knowing where to go, and we earnestly hope that this day will be the day of restoration.

Now, we have found the parents that Heaven has been seeking, brought liberation to the angelic world, and brought liberation to the world of religion and the conscientious world of loyal subjects and kings. However, we also know that the pitiful world of Cain, which has opposed Heaven, religion, and conscience, still remains.

Looking back through history, we see that centered on the Messiah, figures like Judas Iscariot and Emperor Nero, along with communists, are now betraying Heaven. At this time, as we gather the conditions of victory from the universe, we realize that we cannot sweep them away at the judgment seat of Heaven. Therefore, with the name of True Parents, and with the dignified victorious authority you have established, please allow even them to be connected in your name.

Furthermore, we must seek a way to contribute to True Parents and to many religions and conscientious individuals. We earnestly ask you to allow this forever.

In the past, they were the enemies who pierced your heart and killed your beloved son Jesus, but please allow this to become a place of loving our enemies. Open the gates of heaven and earth and spread your loving heart. By liberating them, the gates of hell will open, and the path to abolishing hell will gradually be paved.

Those who stand within such a privilege, whether they are good spirits or the sons and daughters of God, just as they have pledged their loyalty while shedding blood and following the path of death, may they turn back and rebel against the evil world, pledging their loyalty before Heaven, and may this time be one where they vow to gather all evil spirits and evil people to go toward the world you desire, the world God desires.

‘You must be those who pledge that.’ By doing so, we wish to bestow your privileged grace, so may the entire realm of evil spirits, under the leadership of evil, bow before you at this time, before the true True Parents, before the good angelic world, and before the good religious people, pledging to take responsibility for the good direction of Heaven.

Father, loving Father, we earnestly hope that the prayer Jesus prayed while sacrificing his life on the cross will be fulfilled at this time. This history of opposition from the nation and the world of Christianity and the countless forces of Satan over the past 30 years also remains.

However, I do not take them as enemies. When we consider that even the shadow of your providence cannot exist apart from the reality, and that the shadow must follow the reality, I have fought with a heart of loving kindness as True Parents. Please resolve all the injustices of that time. Father, who wishes for forgiveness, please allow it, and may what Jesus desired be fulfilled at this time, releasing what has been bound in your heart.

Surely, we know that Jesus, as he faded away on the path of death, held onto the heart of resentment that only he knew. We also understand that without fulfilling the prayer for his enemies on this earth, you cannot be liberated. Just as the liberation of Jesus and the liberation of Christianity occur at this time, may liberation also occur for all beings that exist centered on you. We offer everything, including all of creation, humanity, the angelic world, and even the countless evil spirits under Satan, in the name of True Parents at this time, and we earnestly hope you will accept it.

To all the countless saints in the spirit world who are with you, centered on the 24 elders and all the good religious people belonging to your throne, we earnestly appeal to you to forgive all the sorrowful facts of the past.

We know that this event will prepare a new turning point in the midst of the world's chaos, raising the banner of victory for Heaven. You know this too. On May 1, 1975, at 8:50, please announce this to the entire universe by your command. Proclaim, ‘I, with the name of God, rejoice in the restoration of the angelic world. I rejoice in the restoration of True Parents. I rejoice in restoring the religions that have been sacrificed until now centered on True Parents. Moreover, I rejoice in fulfilling the wishes of all loyal subjects, kings, and conscientious individuals on earth. I also rejoice in forgetting the pitiful resentment of the world of evil and liberating them.’ I earnestly hope you will make this proclamation in your name.

Now, this child, this son and daughter, receive your proclamation and, with the name of God and the name of True Parents, declare this day of total restoration in your name. All beings must comply with this proclamation and adhere to the laws of Heaven. All nations, all peoples, all spirit worlds, good spirits, and good people must comply, and even those who have been evil can return to the path of restoration, complying with their own standards to return to your embrace. We wish to open this path at this time, so please grant it with both hands.

Therefore, from now on, we will have a ceremony to fulfill such conditions, so Father, please bestow your joyful heart and love, and now extend your authority to suppress evil with goodness, allowing the restoration of Cain and Abel in the original Eden to be fulfilled through this nation and the world. We earnestly hope that on this day, the communist world will bow its head before the path Heaven is taking and comply with the banner of victory.

Yesterday, as Vietnam succumbed to the communist world, may Heaven use it as a sacrifice representing the entire world of Satan, preparing a condition for the communist world to submit to Korea and the world. We earnestly hope for this.

Now, mobilizing the name of God, the angelic world, True Parents, and all good spirits, we proclaim this work, so may countless spirits and conscientious people be mobilized to firmly establish this centered on God!

Today, in this land of Cheongpyeong, may all the spirit world, all the angelic world, God, True Parents on earth, countless Christians, and all other religions, many good nations, and good loyal subjects, and many children witness this day, and may it be a day when we can all embrace you in your arms. We earnestly hope you will accept this as a day of total restoration. We sincerely request that you accept this sequential ceremony as your soul and the foundation of your victory. We pray all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen.

We have had a joyful day in heaven, a joyful day on earth, a joyful day for all creation, a joyful day for all humanity, a joyful day in the spirit world, a joyful day for True Parents, and a joyful day for the Father, and we give thanks and praise for this. We are grateful for the grace that allows us to share all these joyful days, to share all these banquet tables as objects of joy in a celebration like today. We bless in the name of True Parents. Amen.

2) Life of Serving
In the future, long-time members of our Unification Church will likely step onto the international stage. At such times, you must understand that it is a time to practice the life of serving.
Those who live a life of serving receive God's love.
So, who should we serve first? We must serve God. What is the purpose of serving God? Ultimately, it is for our own well-being. To do well, what must we do? We must receive God's love. Without receiving God's love, no matter how much one tries externally to do well, one cannot succeed without being a person in whom God's love can dwell.
Until today, the Unification Church has walked a difficult path amid persecution, but the reason it has not perished and has developed until now is because it has been within God's will, and thus has been in a position to receive God's love. A group or person that receives God's love is protected by God. Right? Isn't that true? A loving parent always thinks of their beloved child, even if the child does not realize it. Isn't that the case in the world? In a marriage, even if one spouse does not know, the other thinks of them, prays for them, and tries to help in every possible way. This is how the love between couples creates a bond.
The same goes for a nation. When there is love for the nation, that love moves the citizens to receive blessings through that person. Citizens receive blessings because of those who love their nation. Therefore, we should hope that all citizens of that nation become patriots. When there are more patriots, that nation thrives. Why is that? Because, by God's love, all beings in a nation were born under God's love and protection.
Thus, beings who are loved by God are drawn to Him without realizing it. People are drawn to Him, money is drawn to Him, and all beings in creation are drawn to Him. Of course, this is true in the physical world, but it is also true in the spiritual world.
It is. Therefore, as you receive more and more of God's love, it grows, and automatically, you can become a central individual or a group. If you have laid the foundation to receive love through the people, then you can become a nation that can move the world.

Because this is a principle, you must live a life of devotion. The question of why you should live a life of devotion is that it is to receive God's love.

Therefore, you must first welcome God. You must welcome God. How should you receive God's love? Since God brings perfect love to us humans, we must invest something perfect. There is a Korean proverb that says, "If you put in sincerity, heaven will respond." This means that it is through heavenly principles. The sincerity means that you give your all, both inside and out. All actions, thoughts, and every aspect of our conscience must be combined and offered. That is sincerity. 'Jeong(정)' refers to spirit. 'Seong(성)' is formed from 'word(언)' and 'to achieve(성).' Therefore, it means to achieve everything inside and out and offer it. Only then can you touch heaven. When heaven is moved, what happens? It thinks of that person, and not only thinks but if that thought remains, love will come. When the thoughts of the whole are concentrated there, love connects here. Isn't that right? When you think, your heart moves.

Therefore, you must stand in a position of sincerity to receive God's love. This is how it works. Just as God loves us humans, if you dedicate everything sincerely for God, you can love God through the feeling of receiving God's love.

Originally, because of the Fall, you cannot love God by yourself. Therefore, through your sincerity for God, God's love comes to you, and through that love, you can know God and love God. The source of love is God.

The way fallen humans can receive God's love is only possible through religion. If we examine the history of love, love originated from God, but where did it move to? Looking back at the time of Adam and Eve, it was transferred to Adam. Through Adam, the history of love has been connected. What this means is that God's love has been connected through the Father. Then, that love through the Father is transferred through the Mother. This continues, and the love of the mother and father combines to bear fruit. By becoming one, you can have the original deep love of God.

In the place where two people, a couple, love and receive love from each other, they can finally become the second protagonists of love; this is the principle. The first protagonist of love is God, but the second protagonist of love begins with Adam and Eve becoming parents. Therefore, parents are the second protagonists of love.

Thus, the history of love flows from God to parents and then to children. This is the traditional history from which original love originated. 

So how should we receive this love of God? This is the question. Until now, people have believed in religion to be saved, but what does salvation mean? It means receiving God's love. To do that, whom have you believed in? Until now, you have believed in a leader. There is a leader of that religion. What does that leader do? Humans have lost their parents because of the Fall. They are like orphans wandering around. Because of this, without receiving love from God as a substitute for parents, they cannot enter the realm of heavenly love and the way of inner salvation. Therefore, by sending such leaders, instead of receiving God's love, they are placed in the position of sons, fulfilling the paternal mission. Ultimately, religion aims to enter into the realm of God's love.

The Unification Church is a religion that can practice a life of devotion based on the foundation of the perfection of spirit and body. Especially in Christianity, this is established. The Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit… Jesus came believing in the Father and the Mother centered on the Holy Spirit, which is remarkable. This shows that this is not merely a human endeavor. Heaven has established a religious form on earth that can realize all these ideals of love, but it has allowed the form of the second God, the protagonist of love, to remain, which is Christianity. Therefore, the logic that Christianity can become the center of all religions is established here.

Thus, the providence of God's love comes through this origin, and today, what the members of the Unification Church believe is to believe in God and to serve the parents centered on spirit and body. This is a remarkable thing.

What is the highest hope for spirits in the spirit world and humans on earth? It is to receive God's love. What is the greatest wish? It is to receive God's love. However, until now, in Christianity, the standards of the spirit world have been divided. Until now, no matter how much humans sought parents who could receive God's love in the reality of spirit and body, they could not find them. However, now in the era of the Unification Church, it is a remarkable fact that we can have the origin of such parents centered on spirit and body.

Therefore, who is the responsible person who can bridge God's love to a perfect stage on this earth? It is the coming Lord. The coming Lord is the protagonist on this earth. Then, what does the protagonist act with? Not with weapons, not with power, not with words. It is love, love. When the character is perfected from the standpoint of recognized love, it resonates everywhere, transcending time. There is no place where it does not resonate, whether in the spirit world, the royal palace, or the earthly world.

In this light, all humanity today is looking for the coming protagonist. Who is that protagonist? It is the Father and Mother. Therefore, in Christianity, it has concluded well that the bridegroom and bride are the conclusion. So, who is the coming Lord? He comes as the Father, and who is the bride? She appears as the Mother. When that is manifested with substance, God's love finally begins through them.

Today, we in the Unification Church believe in order to receive God's love, how should we believe? How should we believe? Now, centered on God's love, if the true parents stand in the position of the second protagonist of love on the foundation of the perfection of spirit and body, we conclude that there is no other way but to dedicate our sincerity centered on the true parents.

What is this life? It is the life of devotion that the Unification Church speaks of. In the past, people offered sincerity to God spiritually, but today, it is about showing filial piety before the substantial parents. Therefore, today, serving parents from a flat position on this earth and showing filial piety to God is a value that can inherit the loyalty of the nation's loyal subjects and the way of the world's saints. That is why, before God or true parents, to have the name of a filial child and to receive the recognition of a filial child is a great and remarkable thing. If you stand in that position, even Jesus would envy you, and you should know that any leader of history would envy you.

Just as God cannot do it, no one can do it. When you are sincere and become one with true parents, no one can follow this. By having the most sincere foundation that only I can have, what happens? God's love comes to dwell within you through your parents.

By standing in such a position, you can finally have love centered on God, centered on God's love, Adam and Eve, and true parents, and thus love can dwell before you, and through that, you can achieve the completion of the ideal family. This is the position of devotion in the Unification Church. Do you understand? There is no other way.

Now, you must receive God's love. Do you understand? What is the way to receive God's love? It is principled, principled. God's love begins from Adam and Eve. So what is the most interesting thing? It is the words of the parents, the stories that parents tell. Isn't that right? Also, what do parents love the most? Then where is heaven? It does not fall from the sky. Heaven is the stage of life shared between parents and children, and it is a place where we can utilize all created beings centered on our lives and our ideals, enjoying the fun of life to the fullest. Do you understand? Heaven is not separate.

That is why, when you work, how good it is to do it for your parents. You must know that. **A New Future for Humanity**  
- Words from the Great Festival of Hope in Daejeon -

<Words> This evening, I sincerely thank the citizens of Daejeon who have gathered here, as well as the many citizens outside due to the cramped space.

I apologize for the unexpected disturbance caused by foreign young men and women who have come to this quiet city of Daejeon over the past few days.

I believe many of you have been quite curious about the person responsible for initiating such events. That very person has appeared here; though not particularly handsome, I sincerely hope that the pure and generous nature of the citizens of Daejeon will embrace me this evening. (Applause)

The theme I wish to contemplate with you this evening is "A New Future for Humanity" or "A New Hope for Humanity." I wish to discuss this topic with the citizens of Daejeon.

The problems of humanity in chaos must be resolved based on a clear view of God. We are currently facing a world that is extremely chaotic. Moreover, we know that this world is filled with strife and distrust. In this current situation, many people are saying that we are in an era of de-ideologization or an era where values are collapsing.

Furthermore, religious people are saying, "This is truly the end. The end of the world has come." This is true from the individual to the family, from nation to nation, and even globally. Thus, we are facing a world that can only lead to despair.

In such times, pursuing a new future means discovering a central ideology that can be welcomed by individuals, families, societies, nations, and the entire world. 

If we briefly look at past history, we see that the uncertain theocentric ideology led the medieval era, but with the collapse of that theocentric thought, humanism emerged. We know that this humanistic era has also failed to fulfill its responsibilities and has now entered a highly dangerous era dominated by materialism. This materialistic thought, akin to materialistic ideology, suggests that we are in an age of the end.

All these problems, including the collapse of values and de-ideologization, arise from the attempt to handle everything centered on humanity.

Therefore, in pursuing this new future, if there is a way to address all these issues, it lies in clearly elucidating whether God exists beyond humanity, whether there is an absolute God or not. In other words, unless we discover what God's perspective is, rather than the human perspective, a new world of hope for humanity cannot come.

Based on a clear view of God, we must address the questions of what life is and what matter is. These issues cannot be dealt with separately; they must be resolved within the governance of a central absolute being.

**Proving God's Reality through the Human Body**  
Here, many people, including elderly grandmothers and grandfathers, have gathered. The question of whether God exists is a serious one, and I would like to express it in a way that is easy to understand.

As you know, humanity has struggled with thoughts, existence, spirit, matter, and God or non-God. Therefore, when the question of whether God exists or not is clarified, all these issues will be resolved.

So, is thought prior to existence? Is matter prior, or is spirit prior? This is a question we cannot overlook.

The most central part of humanity is undoubtedly our eyes, located in the center of our face. I apologize for my hoarse voice. When we think about our eyes, if we ask where the history of the eyes comes from, we would say, "Where does it come from? It comes from my mother and father." Then, where do the eyes of our mother and father come from? We would keep tracing back to our ancestors until we reach our ultimate ancestor.

Today, Christians believe that the ultimate ancestor is Adam and Eve, but regardless of the name, we trace back to the time when our human ancestors were born on this planet.

When we consider the eyes of our grandfather, Adam, those eyes are material. When those eyes were born, did they know that there was a sun in the sky? Did they not? Just think about it for a moment.

Did the eyes themselves know that if they were to be born, they would see the sun in the sky? Did they know that they needed to adjust the light like a camera's aperture? When we ask this, anyone would answer, "Well, of course not. They didn't know." They cannot know.

Furthermore, did the eyes know that there is radiant heat in the atmosphere that causes the moisture in the eyes to evaporate? If we ask this, the eyes themselves cannot know.

The reason our eyes blink is that the moisture in the eyes evaporates. If you keep your eyes open for about 30 minutes, it would be a big problem. Therefore, there must be a mechanism to moisten the eyes. We know that the blinking of the eyes is to replenish the moisture that evaporates. But could the eyes of our ultimate ancestor have known that water evaporates in this spatial world? There is no need to ask; they could not know.

Moreover, there is air on this planet, and when the wind blows, the air moves. This movement causes dust, and if it enters the eyes, it would be a big problem. Therefore, there must be a mechanism to prevent that dust, which is the eyelashes. Isn't that interesting? You have well-placed eyelashes, right? But could the eyes themselves say, "When I appear on earth, there will definitely be air, so eyelashes, come out!"?

When we think about whether the eyes could operate based on astronomical knowledge and the vast phenomena of the physical world without violating any laws, we realize that the eyes themselves cannot do that.

You see, when you have eye pain, you go to the doctor, right? There are so many eye doctors in this world. Even if hundreds of thousands of eye doctors gather, they still have not discovered the mysteries of the eye. The eye is a treasure trove of immense knowledge.

When we ask whether this material eye could be born while controlling the contents of natural history, the answer is no. It cannot happen that way.

Therefore, it is reasonable to conclude that before the eyes came into being, the sun existed, and before the eyes came into being, there was air, and before the eyes came into being, there was a being that understood that moisture evaporates.

So, when we consider whether the existence of the eyes came first or the fundamental reason for the eyes to come into being came first, we cannot overlook the question of whether spirit came first or matter, whether God came first or non-God. Here, we can confidently say that there is a being who knew all these things before the eyes of our ultimate ancestor came into existence. Who is that being? The name does not matter. In Korean, we call Him 하나님, in Japanese, 神様 (kami-sama), in English, God; it doesn't matter what name we use. We can conclude this through simple analogies.

Moreover, the eyes knew that humans could stand and walk. Look at the ears. They are well organized with three mountain ranges, right? Now look at the nose. What if the nose was narrow at the bottom and wide at the top? Wouldn't that be a disaster? Why isn't it turned upside down? Do you know why it is wide at the bottom? It is because of the precious opening of the mouth. When a standing human sweats, if the bottom is narrow, everything would go into the mouth, so we see a fence set up to prevent that from happening.

When we look at the forms of all existence, we cannot deny that they did not come about by mere chance but rather existed based on a vast foundation of knowledge and thought.

From that perspective, we conclude that spirit existed before matter. We conclude that God, who is eternal, unique, and unchanging, exists beyond the incomplete and imperfect nature of humanity. 

**Where True Love, Ideals, Peace, Happiness, and Freedom Come From**  
Humans, regardless of gender or age, have always sought true love. They have pursued true, unchanging love, eternal love, and immutable love, while simultaneously seeking true ideals.

Moreover, they have sought true happiness, true peace, and true freedom. Even now, we are pursuing these in our desperate and difficult reality. However, where does the cause lie for not being able to fulfill all of these? What is wrong? No matter how hard humans try, they cannot find these.

True love does not come from humanity. If there is an absolute God, it comes from God. True ideals do not come from humanity but from the absolute God. True peace, true happiness, and true freedom do not come from humanity but from the true God. Therefore, humans who do not stand in a position that aligns with God's will cannot reach those places.

In this way, imperfect and incomplete humans, who are easily changeable, exist beyond the eternal, unique, and unchanging absolute being. Only through the principles of true love and true ideals presented by that absolute being can we find the ideal conditions for true peace, true happiness, and true freedom.

From this perspective, we must recognize that there is no way for humanity, which has already suffered and made various efforts, to follow the demands of ideals regarding individuals, families, nations, and the world without returning to God and discovering the path that God presents.

This is a significant issue that knowledgeable people, religious individuals, and all humanity living on this planet must discover and resolve together.

From this perspective, when we consider whether love, ideals, happiness, and peace can be spoken of alone, we realize that they cannot be. Can one love alone? Can one claim to have ideals alone? If I take a tiny piece of dust and recite poetry and sing songs about it, thinking it is wonderful, you would see that as normal behavior.

But if I were to laugh and recite poetry alone without anyone else around, what would that be called? They would say I have lost my mind. Therefore, we must understand how precious the existence of the other is.

From this perspective, we cannot deny that words like love, ideals, happiness, peace, and freedom cannot be established alone; they must be established under relative conditions. Do you understand?

**I am the Being that Realizes True Love, Ideals, Peace, and Happiness of God**  
From this perspective, if there is an absolute God, can that God alone say, "Ah, this is love"? Can God alone say, "I have ideals. I am happy. I am the center of peace"? That cannot be established. We must recognize that a counterpart is absolutely necessary.

No matter how omniscient and omnipotent God is, who created and governs the entire universe, without a counterpart, God cannot realize love, and without humans, ideals, happiness, and peace cannot be achieved. This is the most logical conclusion. (Applause)

Then, when we look at this planet, what kind of being can be a counterpart to that absolute God? Today, some scholars say it is monkeys, but can they be a counterpart? You see, monkeys are quite sacred in the zoo, right? Some zoologists say that humans are descended from monkeys, but then we could ask that scholar, "Teacher, who is your grandfather? Is it a monkey?"
So, try greeting the teacher who is a descendant of several dozen generations of monkeys. 
Do you like it? Not a chance. It's an unpleasant thing. Everyone, would you like it if a monkey were your grandfather? 
On this earth, we did not realize this amazing fact that the only beings that can stand before the absolute God are humans among all things. It must be humans. No matter how powerful God is, to fulfill that love, it cannot be done without humans. 
Until now, you have understood the value of humans as worthless. 
“Oh, I’m just a nameless farmer living in this rural area, living and dying like a clod of dirt.” Have you realized that your existence is absolutely necessary to fulfill God's ideal condition? We did not know this.

What would the answer be? The young ladies are smiling in agreement. The formula of cosmic creation 
God is the King of Wisdom. God is also the King of Love, the King of Ideals, and the King of Peace, Happiness, and Freedom. If God only thought of Himself, would He have created heaven and earth? The term creation refers to the input of power. If there is an artist in this world, that artist wishes to create a masterpiece. To create a masterpiece, the artist invests all their mind and all their sincerity. Only through complete investment can a perfect masterpiece emerge. It cannot be an incomplete investment. Only through complete investment can a masterpiece come into being. 
What is the essence of God’s creation? Today, established believers think, “God is omniscient and omnipotent, so He created by His word,” and they believe it was done like magic. No, it is not. He had to invest all His intelligence and all of Himself in this endeavor. That is why He loves. Can you love something without investing effort, blood, and flesh? It is because He invested His bone of bones, flesh of flesh, thought of thoughts, and all of Himself that He can take it as an object of hope. 
Therefore, the creation itself began from investment. Power must be invested. Nothing comes into existence without investment. It is the same. Based on the principle that a complete object is established through complete investment, God’s relationship with the object is a complete investment. 
In other words, God did not exist for Himself; the act of creation began as a movement to exist for the object. The history of creation is the act of standing in a position to exist for the object. (Cheers and applause) 
This is the principle of the creation of heaven and earth, so where does God place the ideal starting point? It is not to have everything for Himself. It is not about saying, “You, come to me and cling to me.” It is about investment. It is not about clinging. It is about investment. It is about reducing oneself. In other words, we can conclude that the principle of existing for the sake of others has been established here. 
Therefore, God has invested for humans. In other words, God Himself exists for humans. We must understand this fact. We must recognize that He has been continuously existing for the sake of humans. We can conclude here that He governs the rights of life and death for the sake of humans. (Applause) 
From here, we have learned that true love is established only in existing for the sake of others. Everyone, what is the Fall? It is the opposite of this. If you do not repay me, you must repay it before the nation and the world. That is it. 

If you have put your name down to build a church, you must repay more for the nation and the world and develop this, right? Is that not so? If you helped build one, it is entirely justifiable to build two or three more. Do you understand? "Yes." Those who understand correctly, raise your hands. Those who understand, raise your hands. Now, put them down. Then, in a short time, we must restore three churches in one district. 

The tradition of the Unification Church has been established by the teacher. You did not establish it, but the tradition of going from the individual to the family, from the tribe to the nation, and to the world has already been established by the teacher of the Unification Church. Do you understand? So, when I say to resemble someone, it does not mean to resemble my face as it is. The path of the providence must be followed. Do you understand? 

Therefore, since the teacher has led the global fortune to the global era, you must inherit that awareness and thought and become the teacher's representatives. You must become representatives. Until now, you have not been representatives. Until now, you have not even been able to be representatives. 

Now that you have a foundation and a church, you can assert authority and prestige there, and depending on your efforts, you will encounter a time when you can thrive in every way. Just because there is no subjective church does not mean I will build a church for you and then create an environment that does not oppose it. I am doing that now. Because of this Hope Day grand feast, I feel like many ice mountains are breaking in front of the path of our Unification Church, welcoming spring and beginning to melt. Do you feel that? "Yes." 

From now on, you must have a higher level of determination than when you entered the Unification Church. When you entered before, you were happy by yourself, but now you must be able to rejoice with the church at a higher level. You must regain that timid spirit of 'let's go!' from when you entered, and during the days of running for three years, you must see it as crossing the boundaries of this nation. That is the teacher's perspective. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 

Now, the 172 of you must unite and become the teacher's representatives and fight horizontally. There is no indemnity in fighting horizontally. In the past, how did you all end up? You were centered here. To be the center of the district, you needed roots. You had to live individually like this, but now you are all grafted and connected before this center. Do you understand? 

Because you are connected like that, when you act, you can grow immensely. When you act with the teacher, this great army can spread out like this and go like this. Depending on your actions, heavenly fortune.... What should I say, drainage pipes, you know? Just like drainage pipes, if you make your drainage pipe big, a lot of water will come out, and if you make it small, only a proportional amount of water will come out. You must understand that. Do you understand? "Yes." The church can be seen as a transformer. When you flip the switch, all the villages should light up. This house is a Unification Church, this house is a Unification Church, and the time will come when all the Unification Church bulbs will light up.

So, if you say, 'Great!' and someone asks, 'Why is it great?' and you open your eyes wide and say, 'What? He is not greater than you....' then everyone will fall over. So, it has become a good time to work. Do you understand? "Yes." 

In this era, one thing we must hold is the subjectivity. We must resolve not to become indebted to foreign members and must overcome this time. That is why I have helped you in my name. Do you understand? I have helped you in my name. I do not help in the name of foreigners. Until now, I have helped you in my name, so if I have money that I can use as I please, and I give it to the poor Korean people because they look pitiful, that does not fall under conditions. Do you understand? If I gave it to someone who threatened or blackmailed me, that would fall under conditions, but I must give it to the poor Korean people with the money I can use and spare. That is why I think building churches is the best way to do so, as I believe that if I build a church, I will not fall under conditions. I think from that perspective. 

However, one thing is that until that money comes out, heaven is mobilized, the teacher is mobilized, and all members are mobilized with this blood, sweat, and tears behind it. In the church, by being called as a thousand people or ten thousand people, we can take a leap as a nation, and if we utilize it as a point where we can become a tribal center and a national center, it will become the way to the world where all sincerity is established. Have you all contributed even a little to the Day of Hope Festival? Did you or not? "A little." A little? That's just for your own sake, isn't it? How can that be a contribution? The teacher has said unpleasant things to you until now, but now that I am helping you and doing all this, aren't you grateful? "Yes." "That's right." Right? "Yes." When I return, will I definitely do that, or not? "I will do that." You all answer well. I can relieve my feelings of disappointment by saying this. 168   천운과 우리의 사명
비로소 그것이 가정의 기점이 되어 가지고 가정적 7년노정이 된 거예요. 
선생님은 개인적인 승리의 기반을 닦아 가지고 민족의 한계선을 넘어왔지
만은 어머님은 그렇지가 않다구요. 그러니 어머님을 재창조해야 된다구요. 
이것이 제1차 7년노정이에요. 제1차 7년노정은 뭣이냐 하면, 상대적인 면
에 있는 어머니를 중심삼아 다시 기르는 기간입니다. 해와는 아담을 통해
서 창조된 거라구요. 그러므로 아담은 해와를 창조해 내지 않으면 안 되는 
것입니다.
그렇기 때문에 아무것도 모르는 어머니를, 여기에 있어서 안됐지만 미안
합니다. (어머니를 보시면서 웃으심) 모셔다가 철부지한 걸 백방으로 한 
목적을 지녀 가지고 파란곡절을 다 겪게 하여 어머니로서 거쳐야 할 십자
가의 모든 고비 길을 다 거치게 한 거라구요. 3분의 2는 내가 지는 거라구
요. 사탄이가 빼앗았던 3분의 2를 내가 지고 어머니의 3분의 1의 소생․
장성․완성을 중심삼고 나온 거예요. 그것은 거꾸로 끌려가니 끌려가게 돼 
있다구요. 그러니까 싫더라도 순응하며 싫더라도 이를 악물고 혓바닥을 깨
물면서 남편이 가는 길을 간 것입니다. 이것이 우리 한국의 고유사상이요, 
동방예의지국이라고 하는 그 나라의 한 여자가 지니고 가야 할 품성인 것
을 알고 어떤 충신의 아내보다도, 어떤 군왕의 아내보다도 순응할 수 있는 
마음을 가지고 묵묵히 따라와야 된다는 거예요.
이럼으로 말미암아 개인시대를 지나고 가정시대를 거쳐 나가야 돼요. 그
러면서 여러분들은 횡적인 가정투쟁을 하는 거예요. 그다음부터는 축복을 
해주면서 횡적인 개인투쟁시대, 횡적인 가정투쟁시대로 이렇게 자꾸 크는 
거라구요. 그다음에는 횡적인 종족투쟁시대로서 확대되는 거예요. 그러한 
기반을 중심삼고 보니, 예수님이 비로소 이스라엘 유대교가 믿는 자리에서 
유대교의 중심의 어떠한 귀갓집 딸과 결혼한 자리를 대신했다 할 수 있는 
조건이 된다는 거예요. 그러므로 종족 기반이 없으면 안 된다구요.
그러면서 36가정으로부터 72가정과 120가정까지 3년 동안 축복을 해

2차 7년노정이에요. 그러므로 2차 7년노정은 본래 선생님이 일하는 것이

아니고 여러분이 일해야 됩니다. 2차 7년노정은 축복가정을 중심삼아 가지
고 횡적으로 연결되어야 하는 때예요. 이래서 하나의 중심점을 중심삼아 
가지고 여러분은 죽으나 사나 어떠한 명령이든지 선생님의 가정을 중심삼
고 철석같이 뭉쳐야 돼요. 여기에 반대하고 다 이러는 것은 전부 다 앞으
로 후대에 법도 조건에 다 걸린다구요. 선생님 앞에서 다시 용서받지 않고
는 저나라에 들어갈 길이 없다는 거라구요.
그래서 2차 7년노정은 이러한 중심을 중심삼아 가지고 비로소 이 종족
이 벗어나는 거예요. 종족이 벗어나기 위해서는 이 부모님을 기반으로 해
야 됩니다. 이스라엘 민족과 이스라엘 나라의 사람들은 본래 국가를 만들
어 가지고 부모님을 위해야 예수님을 맞을 수 있었다구요. 알겠어요? 무슨 
말인지 알겠어요?「예.」본래의 이스라엘 민족, 그 가정들은 전부 다 나라
를 수습해 가지고 예수님을 모셔야 된다 그 말이라구요. 그래서 수습된 나
라 기반과 교회 기반과 종족 기반 위에서 예수님의 축복의 날을 중심삼고 
잔치를 해야 되는 거라구요. 알겠어요? 그런데 그렇게 되지 못하고 까꿀잽
이가 되었다구요.
그렇기 때문에, 선생님의 가정을 중심삼고 여러분이 뭘 해야 되느냐? 가
정적으로 민족을 수습하고 새로운 민족이 ‘앞으로 이 국가가 가야 할 길은,
‘이 민족이 이렇게 가지 않으면 안 된다.’는 입장을 세워 가지고 새로운 주
체사상을 세워서 이 민족이 관심을 가질 수 있는 길로 몰아넣어야 된다는 
것입니다. 알겠어요? 그래서 이 2차 7년노정은 가정을 중심삼은 전국 확대 
활동시대라는 거예요. 알겠어요?「예.」
여러분들이 1970년도, 71년도, 72년도에 3년노정을 갔지요? 이 2년 8
개월 동안을 중심삼아 가지고 무엇을 해야 되느냐 하면, 앞으로 2차 7년노
정이 끝나기 전에 여러분들이 이 민족 앞에 가정으로서 갈 수 있는 책임을 
다 해 놓아야 됩니다. 축복받은 가정들이 그것 안 하면 안 된다구요. 그래
서 축복받은 가정들에게는 3년노정이 남아 있는 거예요.
예수님이 3년노정 위에 개인으로 한을 풀지 못한 가정적 기반이 연장되
어 있기 때문에, 가정적으로 한(恨)이 맺힌 3년노정을 풀어 드려야 할 사
명이 남아 있습니다. 그러므로 오늘날 축복받은 가정들은 전체 동원시대가 
온 거예요. 36가정에서부터 그런 일이 벌어진 거라구요. 이래 가지고 어떻
171 
게 되느냐 하면, 어머니 아버지가 다 갈라지고 아들딸이 다 갈라지는 거라
구요. 이거 얼마나 비참하냐 말이에요. 타락한 세계에서도 이런 놀음이 없
었다는 거라구요. 타락한 아담 해와가 떨어져 쫓겨 나오게 될 때에도 어머
니 아버지의 주먹에 움켜 가지고 사탄 주관권으로 떨어졌던 것입니다. 그
렇지만 오늘날 하나님을 중심삼은 탕감복귀원칙에 있어서 그 이상 될 수 
있는 가정을 만들려면 가정을 다 헤쳐 버리더라도 사탄 편에서 돌아서 가
지고 하나님을 위한다 할 수 있는 가정적 형태를 만들어야 합니다. 그렇지 
않고는 가정적 해원성사의 기반을 닦을 수 없다고 보는 거라구요. 알겠어
요?
그래서 1970년도에 여러분들의 가정 전체가 국가와 민족 앞에 ‘이렇게 
해야 대한민국이 사는 것이다. 하나님을 위해서 통일교회의 가정 식구들이 
모든 것을 다 버리고 이 나라 이 민족의 장래를 위하여 천륜이 오는 방향
을 이 민족 앞에 오게 하기 위하여 이렇게 간다!’ 하는 방향 제시를 했던 
것입니다.
그럼으로 말미암아 무슨 일이 벌어지느냐 하면, 선생님의 가정시대에 있
어서는 핍박받았다구요. 1차 7년노정은 어머니가 아직까지 그 자리를 못 
넘어갔기 때문에 사탄이 참소할 수 있는 기세가 남아 있었습니다. 그래서 
선생님이나 어머니나 가정이 핍박받아 나왔지만 여러분의 시대는 그런 시
대가 지나간 거라구요. 알겠어요? 알겠어요, 무슨 말인지?「예.」횡적인 면
에서 여러분들이 가정을 중심삼아 가지고 이걸 전부 다 헤쳐 나온 거예요.
이런 놀음을 함으로 말미암아 대한민국이 통일교회를 반대했고, 기성교
회가 통일교회를 반대했다구요. 반대한 민족은 사실 용서받을 수 없는 거
라구요. 그러나 여러분의 가정들 여러분의 아기들을 중심삼아 가지고 헤어
지게 될 때, 자기 어머니 아버지, 혹은 외갓집의 어머니 아버지, 사돈의 8
촌 집까지 전부 다 갖다 맡겼다구요. 그런 놀음 했지요? 그렇게 될 때에 
혹자는 조롱하고 혹자는 저주하고 혹자는 미워했을는지 모르지만, 그 반면
에 혹자들은 그 아기들을 보고 불쌍한 아기라고 하며 그를 사랑하고, 도리
어 어머니가 없다고 눈물을 지으며 기도한 사람도 있다구요. 뜻을 따라오
지는 않지만 이들이 가는 것이 거룩하다고 하면서 그 아이들을 책임지고 
누구보다도 정성들여 가지고 키워 준 사람들도 그 기간에 있기 마련이라는 
172   천운과 우리의 사명
것입니다. 알겠어요? 그런 걸 보면, 축복받은 여러분의 가정의 애기들을 
이 나라 이 민족이, 환난시대에, 싸움시대의 피난 때에 붙들고 사랑해 줬
다는 조건이 있음으로 말미암아 이 민족이 뜻 앞에 벗어난 것을 비로소 접
근시킬 수 있었다는 것입니다. 알겠어요?
다시 말하면, 예수가 태어날 때 환영받지 못한 입장이었지만 그래도 동
정했던 사람이 있었던 것과 마찬가지로, 하늘 앞에 추방되어야 할 민족이 
비로소 그러한 활동을 한 사람으로 말미암아, 여러분을 위하고 자식들을 
위할 수 있는 이런 환경에 연결됨으로써 민족이 용서받을 수 있는 때로 들
어온다는 거예요. 알겠어요?
그래서 3년노정이 끝남으로 말미암아 무슨 일이 벌어지느냐 하면, 민족
이 이 통일교회 앞에 탕감돼요. 이와 같이 가정을 버리고 나라를 버리고 
세계를 위할 수 있는 사상을 가지면 이 나라 이 민족과 세계가 살 수 있다
는 시위, 본을 보여 준 거예요. 이렇게 선생님을 중심삼고 상대적인 면에
서 국가를 대한 탕감조건을 세웠기 때문에, 국가를 넘어갈 수 있는 길이 
벌어진 거라구요. 알겠어요? 그러한 탕감조건을 세워 놓고 세계로 넘어갈 
그런 때가 되었기 때문에 2차 7년노정이 끝나기 전에 선생님은 세계적 무
대를 향한 거예요. 여러분들이 그런 탕감 사명을 국가와 민족을 중심삼고 
했다 하면, 선생님은 세계적 무대로 나가야 돼요. 이건 영적이에요, 영적. 
여러분도 영적이고 다 영적이라구요. 실체적이 아니라구요. 영적으로 해 
나오는 거예요. 
미국을 중심삼은 1972년부터의 3년노정의 의의
만약 예수님이 죽지 않았더라면…. 2차 7년노정까지 이 나라와 완전히 
하나되지 않으면 안 되는 거예요. 원리가 끝나는 거라구요. 그렇지만 예수
님이 죽음으로 말미암아 우리 시대에 있어서의 이것이 도움이 됐다는 걸 
여러분은 알아야 된다구요. 죽음으로 말미암아 영적 주체적인 이런 이념권
을 우리가 민족 앞에 세울 수 있었고 그 누구도 통일교회를 따라올 수 없
는 입장에서 우위에 서 가지고 일어섬으로 말미암아 천륜이 따라오는 것을 
우리 축복가정들이 이어받아 가지고 세계로 연결시킬 수 있는 때가 돌아온 
173 
거예요.
1972년을 중심삼아 선생님이 세계의 7년노정을 따라서 세계적인 기반
을 연결시키지 않으면 안 되겠기 때문에 1971년부터 여기에서 미국에 갈 
것을 준비한 거라구요. 이래 가지고 1972년에 이것과 더불어 연결시켜 나
가면서 세계적 무대로 나간 것이 선생님의 이 미국의 작전이다 이거예요. 
알겠어요? 이래 가지고 3년을 마치고 1974년까지 전세계가 어떻게 되었
느냐 하면, 과거에는 한국에서 기독교 앞에 내가 놀림을 받았고 공격을 받
았지만 이제는 세계의 기독교권을 공격을 하는 거예요.
그러면 국가적 기독교는 세계의 기독교권 내에 포괄되는 것입니다. 알겠
어요?「예.」국가 민족권 내에 있는 기독교가 나를 반대했지만, 내가 세계
적 기독교를 공격할 때 그들이 반대하지 않고 환영하는 승리적 기반을 닦
을 수 있게 된다면, 국가가 아무리 반대하더라도 이 세계의 승리 기반 앞
에 완전히 수습되고 완전히 탕감복귀된다는 거예요. 알겠어요?
예수님이 실체를 쓰고 영․육을 중심삼고 이루었어야 할 3년노정을 이
루지 못했기 때문에, 기독교문화권을 중심삼은 세계도상 3년노정의 기반을 
탕감복귀해야 되는 것이 미국을 중심삼은 1972년부터의 3년노정이라는 
것입니다. 알겠어요?
그래서 1974년까지 완전히 영적 기준 앞에 주체적인 하나님의 섭리의 
주체성을 세울 수 있는 조건을 세웠기 때문에 비로소 한국을 향해서 돌아
올 수 있는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 지금 미국 기독교 가운데에는 통일교
회 레버런 문만이 젊은 사람들을 지도할 수 있다고 하는 사람이 많다구요. 
하나님의 이름 가운데서 공산당을 능가할 수 있고 미국 어떠한 조야의 그 
누가 갖지 못한 천운을 가졌다 하는 이런 주체적인 하나의 기반을 닦고 돌
아온 것이 1974년입니다. 그래서 작년 12월 29일에 일본을 들러 가지고 
돌아왔다구요.
그러면서 그때에 한 것이 뭣이냐 하면, 영국에 가서도 한 쌍을 축복해 
주고 미국에 가서도 한 쌍을 축복해 준 것인데, 한국에 와서도 이런 놀음
을 해 주는 일이 벌어져야 된다는 거예요. 이렇게 연결된 걸 여러분이 알
아야 돼요.
기독교가 영적 구원섭리의 세계적 확대를 했던 것을 비로소 대한민국을 
174   천운과 우리의 사명
중심삼아 가지고, 기독교의 영적 기반을 중심삼고 국가 기준까지 되어 있
던 것에 반드시 육적 기반을 연결시켜야 할 때가 되었기 때문에, 비로소 
대한민국에서 선생님이 실체(實體)를 드러낸 거예요. 알겠어요? 그때까지
는 공석에 나타나 본 적이 없다구요. 알겠어요?
원래는 30대에 선생님이 이 놀음을 했어야 하는 것인데 지금 50대에 
이 놀음을 하고 있어요. 그 기간은 완전히 재탕감기간이었다구요. 그래서 
1차 뱅퀴트(banquet), 2차 합동 결혼식, 3차 기동대를 중심삼아 가지고 1
차에서는 개인적으로 그 누구한테도, 그 누구보다도 드러나는 입장에 서야 
되고, 2차에서는 가정적으로 드러나야 되는 것입니다. 이 민족의 가정을 
초월한 대표적 가정이 되어야 됩니다. 그다음 3차에는 이 민족이 어느 누
구든 따라올 수 없는 세계적인 활동이 될 수 있도록 하는 국제기동대를 투
입해 가지고 활동을 해 나왔습니다. 이랬기 때문에 개인으로, 가정으로, 전
체로 드러날 수 있게 된 것입니다. 이렇게 하면 이 나라 이 민족이 자기도 
모르게 회오리바람 가운데 돌아간다 하는 것과, 천운이 가는 길이 그러한 
길이라는 것을 선생님이 알았기 때문에, 될 것이냐, 아니냐 하는 문제가 
이런 원칙에서 돼야 된다는 것입니다. 반드시 붐을 조성하지 않으면 안 된
다는 것이었어요.
이렇게 조성한 붐을 살려 가지고 어디까지 가야 되느냐? 대한민국 전역
을 휩쓸어야 되는 것입니다. 여기서 새로운 아이디어를 세워 가지고, 만일
에 남북 결렬이 벌어지게 된다면, 우리가 주체적인 책임을 하지 않으면 안 
되는 실체 국가적 책임을 해야 할 입장에 서야 합니다. 그래서 우리가 박

When I, the son of God, am about to die... then it’s okay. I believe that Unification Church members should move forward from that perspective.
Cherish and love all things
Next, we need to be frugal in spending money. Money is also a material thing, right? I am grateful to God for making it so that Koreans can’t live poorly. 
You must know how to spend money wisely. You should save even a penny. If you spend it wrongly, a piece of Korea is consumed. A piece of the world is consumed. Knowing that, you must spend your resources wisely. You should also wear clothes sparingly. The word frugality is born here. From today, it will become a new historical origin... Everything must go to heaven. I hope you understand that all things must head towards heaven.
In our Unification Church, we celebrate four major holidays: Parents’ Day, Children’s Day, Day of All Things, and God’s Day. God’s Day has become the last of them, right? God’s Day has become the most important in the age of blessings. Although it has come to this, in the future, we need to integrate God’s Day, Parents’ Day, Children’s Day, and Day of All Things into a single day of historical commemoration. When that time comes, the democratic world will all converge before the purpose, and the communist world will kneel down, allowing us to offer the victory of this land to God. At that time, because Adam and Eve completed the Garden of Eden, it will be the Day of All Things and the Day of Children, the Day of Children and the Day of All Things, the Day of Parents and the Day of Children, the Day of Parents and the Day of God... We must resolve to go towards establishing such a day, as we still have a path to walk. Do you understand? “Yes.”
Here, all of this is within God’s realm of love, embracing humanity, embracing all things, embracing the angelic world, the spirit world, and moving towards a unified day of victory as a good world. Knowing that we still have a day to go for this, I hope you will commemorate such a day and renew your determination and resolve, as I conclude the words of the teacher. Do you understand?
<Prayer> Beloved Father! Thank you for holding onto us and not letting go as we walk the path of restoration, from the individual age to the family age, through the tribal, national age, and enduring fierce battles. Even when we were sad and lonely, you comforted us and helped us pledge for a day of victory, and we are even more grateful before your holy presence today.
Today marks the 13th Day of All Things. In this Unification altar, where we can praise a victory of a higher dimension in the historical age, Father, we thank you for the path that remains for us to advance into a new light, a new time of glory... into a higher-dimensional world.
Now, it is time to align the direction of all spirit worlds with the direction of humanity on this earth, and to discern the direction of all things on this earth, forming a unified orbit consistent with your heart, so that we can march towards a single purpose. We know that if we stray from your name, we cannot belong to your will.
That is why many true religious people know that they must come under the shade of the Unification Church. Buddhists know that, Confucians know that, and Christians know that. If they do not realize this, a day will come when they will understand the miserable future that awaits them. Knowing that everything concludes according to your providential will, we hope that we will not meet the nation or humanity with the results of sorrow. We sincerely ask and hope that you will protect us and keep us from bringing about such results.
Now, we know that the responsibility to awaken the mission that America must fulfill in the future lies with us.
Now that Korea has crossed a certain threshold, we must rally our full strength centered around America and advance towards the final battleground. We sincerely hope that you will guide us to cross over that hill and lead us as your peace messengers.
With the resolve and hope to do so, we wish to follow you, becoming sons and daughters whom you can remember, whom you can ask, whom you can command, and thus, allow us to be those who are not ashamed to be presented and boasted about before all the world.
We recognize that your will is calling us. We earnestly ask that you allow us to be those who can be faithful and loyal to that will, and we pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
